when N─Бr─Бyaс╣Зa becomes the Redeemer,

├Йl es con Su atributo (Lakс╣гm─л).

English

Arulalap-perumal Emberumanar states :-

" Before understanding the sabstantive which has attributes,
the attributes have to be understood.
Therefore to understand Hari who has Lakс╣гm─л for His attribute,
the attribute, ‘Lakс╣гm─л’, has (first) to be understood."

Espa├▒ol

Arulalap-perumal Emberumanar afirma -

" Antes de comprender el sustantivo que tiene atributos,
los atributos tienen que entenderse.
Por lo tanto, para entender a Hari, quien tiene a Lakс╣гm─л como Su atributo,
el atributo, ‘Lakс╣гm─л’, tiene (primero) que ser comprendido."

рдЗрддреНрдпреН рдПрддрдореН рдЕрд░реНрдердВ рдЪ рд╕рд┐рджреНрдзреЛрдкрд╛рдп-рд╢реЛрдзрдирд╛рдзрд┐рдХрд╛рд░реЛ рд╜рд╡реЛрдЪрд╛рдо рее

English

That this (Lakс╣гm─л) is an attribute both in the first part (of the Dvaya) and in the second
has already been explained in the chapter Siddhop─Бya ┼Ыodhana

as also the principle that
when the up─Бya has an attribute,
there will be no duality of the up─Бya.

Espa├▒ol

Que este (Lakс╣гm─л) es un atributo tanto en la primera parte (del Dvaya) como en la segunda
ya ha sido explicado en el cap├нtulo Siddhop─Бya ┼Ыodhana

como tambi├йn el principio de que
cuando el up─Бya tiene un atributo,

English

The meaning of ┼Ъr─л:-
In the Bhagavat ┼Ы─Бstras (pa├▒car─Бtra),
the word ┼Ъr─л has been etymologically interpreted in six ways:

(1) ┼Ыr─лyate (is resorted to);
(2) ┼Ыrayate (resorts to);
(3) ┼Ыrnoti (listens);
(4) ┼Ыr─Бvayati (makes listen);
(5) ┼Ыrniti (removes);
(6) ┼Ыr─лnati (makes ripe).

Espa├▒ol

El significado de ┼Ъr─л:-
En los Bhagavat ┼Ы─Бstras (pa├▒car─Бtra),
la palabra ┼Ъr─л ha sido etimol├│gicamente interpretada de seis maneras:

(1) ┼Ыr─лyate (se recurre a);
(2) ┼Ыrayate (recurre a);
(3) ┼Ыrnoti (escucha);
(4) ┼Ыr─Бvayati (hace escuchar);
(5) ┼Ыrniti (elimina);
(6) ┼Ыr─лnati (hace madurar).

that Lakс╣гm─л plays the role of a mediator

“O Lakс╣гm─л, with a countenance as delightful as the moon!

(we see) that the essential nature (svar┼лpa) of Bhagav─Бn

which declares Thy Lord as being such and such.”

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

English

while those that are appropriate to Bhagav─Бn’s being the object of attainment
should be borne in mind
in regard to the second part (of Dvaya ).

Espa├▒ol

mientras que aquellos que son apropiados para que Bhagav─Бn sea el objeto de logro
debe tenerse en cuenta
con respecto a la segunda parte (de Dvaya).

English

In the surrender of such as one’s essential Nature (and the burden of protection etc.),
the Master is well known,
to those who see with the eye of the ┼Ыrutis,
as the up─Бya or means and as one to whom the surrender is made.
He is also the upeya (the object of attainment).

Espa├▒ol

En la rendici├│n de la propia Naturaleza esencial (y la carga de la protecci├│n, etc.),
el Maestro es bien conocido,
a aquellos que ven con el ojo de los ┼Ыrutis,
como el up─Бya o significa y como aquel a quien se hace la entrega.
├Йl es tambi├йn el upeya (el objeto de logro).
